<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="classification-of-hypertension">Classification of hypertension<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#classification-of-hypertension" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Pre-hypertension: Systolic BP 120-140 or diastolic BP 80-90.
Stage I hypertension: Systolic BP &gt; 140-160 or diastolic BP &gt;90-100.
Stage II: Systolic BP &gt; 160 or diastolic BP &gt; 100.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="3-temperature">3. TEMPERATURE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#3-temperature" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Sites:</p>
<ul>
<li>Armpit (most used)</li>
<li>Oral - adults &amp; children who can follow instructions</li>
<li>Groin - in children</li>
<li>Rectal - for children and unconscious. Most accurate but uncomfortable.</li>
</ul>
<p>Requirements:</p>
<ul>
<li>Thermometer:</li>
</ul>
<p>0 Mercury
o Electronic
o Inflated auxiliary thermometers
o Low reading thermometer</p>
<ul>
<li>A container containing cotton soaked in disinfectant. Change disinfectant every 24 hours</li>
<li>A quick assessment of temperature can be done by use of back of the hand.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="4-respiratory-rate">4. RESPIRATORY RATE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#4-respiratory-rate" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Note character and rhythm.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="1-obstetric-abdominal-examination">1. OBSTETRIC ABDOMINAL EXAMINATION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#1-obstetric-abdominal-examination" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Regular abdominal examination is an important component of both antenatal care and monitoring labour</p>
<p>By abdominal examination you can ascertain:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>The size of the uterus and note whether it corresponds to the period of amenorrhea</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The size of the foetus</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The lie presentation and attitude of the foetus</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The relative sizes of the brim of the pelvis and the presenting part</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Whether the foetus is alive</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The presence of the abnormal condition eg excess liquor amnii, twin pregnancy, abdominal tumours</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="requirements">Requirements<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#requirements" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Foetoscope</li>
<li>Watch with second hand</li>
<li>A bowl with dry gauze and cotton swabs</li>
<li>Tape measure</li>
<li>Receiver for the dirty swabs</li>
<li>Couch</li>
<li>Bed sheet</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="examination">Examination<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#examination" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Explain the procedure to the patient
Ensure privacy
Wash and dry your hands to ensure they are warm
Expose the abdomen</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="inspection">Inspection<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#inspection" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Inspect for shape, size, skin, linear nigra, striae gravidarum, scars, foetal movements, umbilicus</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="palpation">Palpation<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#palpation" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="leopold-s-maneuver">LEOPOLD'S MANEUVER<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#leopold-s-maneuver" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251214-fc8fe05c.jpeg" alt="img-8.jpeg"></p>
<ul>
<li>First maneuver: Fundal Grip</li>
<li>Second maneuver: Umbilical Grip</li>
<li>Third maneuver: (1st pelvic grip) = The Pawlick's Grip,</li>
<li>Fourth maneuver: (2nd Pelvic Grip) = pelvic grip</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="first-leopold-s-maneuver-fundal-grip">First Leopold's maneuver: Fundal Grip<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#first-leopold-s-maneuver-fundal-grip" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Facing the mother, palpate the fundus with both hands</p>
<ul>
<li>Assess for shape, size, consistency and mobility</li>
</ul>
<p>Fetal head: firm, hard, and round</p>
<ul>
<li>Moves independently of the rest</li>
<li>Detectable by ballottement</li>
</ul>
<p>Breech/buttocks: softer and has bony prominences</p>
<ul>
<li>Moves with the rest of the form</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="fundal-height">Fundal height<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#fundal-height" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Using your left hand, place either the ulnar/radial border of the index finger on the abdomen from xiphisternum</li>
<li>Apply pressure as you move downwards in steps to locate the underlying mass</li>
<li>Once the mass is encountered maintain the hand or finger at that level</li>
<li>Using the right hand, determine the number of fingerbreaths from the superior border of the umbilicus up to the level of fundus</li>
<li>Each finger breath multiplied by 2. Fundal height at umbilicus is 22/40, at sympysis pubis is <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>12</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mn>40</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">12 / 40</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">12/40</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li>Alternatively you can use tape measure to check fundal height from symphysis pubis through umbilicus to xiphoid sternum. Note the fundal height</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="second-leopold-s-maneuver-determine-position-of-the-back-lie">Second Leopold's maneuver - Determine position of the back (lie)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#second-leopold-s-maneuver-determine-position-of-the-back-lie" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Lie is the relation of the baby's long axis to the mother's uterus long axis
Still facing the mother, place both palms on the abdomen
Hold right hand still and with deep but gentle pressure, use left hand to feel for the firm, smooth back. Repeat using opposite hands</p>
<p>Feel for:
The foetal poles
Regularity or irregularity and convexity
Absence of foetal poles in the flanks = longitudinal lie
Presence of foetal poles on the flanks = transverse lie (long axis of the fetus is perpendicular to that of the mother's)</p>
<p>Oblique lie = long axis of the fetus is 0-90 degrees (or 90-180 degrees) to that of the mother's</p>
<p>Uniform, firm convexity of contour = side of the foetal back</p>
<ul>
<li>Determine whether convex contour is nearer the front or far out in the flank gives idea about position</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="third-leopold-s-maneuver-presentation">Third Leopold's Maneuver - presentation<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#third-leopold-s-maneuver-presentation" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Determine what part is lying above the inlet.</li>
<li>Using the right hand apply the pawlik's grip (single handed palpation) to fell the part of foetus overlying the pelvic inlet</li>
<li>If transverse, any mass felt is most likely the shoulder = shoulder presentation</li>
<li>If longitudinal lie differentiate between cephalic and breech presentation. A hard rounded mass indicates cephalic presentation</li>
<li>Pawlick's grip gives precise findings when head is not engaged</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="fourth-leopold-s-maneuver-engagement">Fourth leopold's maneuver - engagement<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#fourth-leopold-s-maneuver-engagement" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Engagement is checked while facing the mothers lower limbs and with both hands placed on the lower abdomen</li>
<li>If the fingers seem to meet below the presenting part then engagement has not occurred. When engagement occurs, the head will be fixed on the pelvis</li>
<li>Before deep engagement, as the fingers are passed down the presenting part, the area that is most prominent on the head is noted.</li>
<li>If the cephalic prominence is on the side of the small parts (limbs), it implies the head is well flexed hence Vertex presentation</li>
<li>If prominence is felt equally on both sides - deflexed hence brow presentation</li>
<li>If prominence is on the side opposite that with the small parts and indistinct back curvature, the findings suggest face presentation.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="attitude">Attitude<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#attitude" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Refers to the position of the foetal head to its trunk.</li>
<li>The normal position is complete flexion giving vertex presentation</li>
<li>When deflexion = brow presentation</li>
</ul>
<p>When extension = face presentation</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="denominator">DENOMINATOR<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#denominator" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Denominator is the arbitrary point on the presenting part used as a point of reference in denoting the position of the presenting part in relation to the pelvis.</p>
<ul>
<li>Vertex presentation - the denominator is OCCIPUT</li>
<li>Brow presentation - the denominator is sinciput</li>
<li>Face presentation - the denominator is mentum or chin</li>
<li>Breech presentation - the denominator is sacrum</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="position">Position<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#position" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Relation of denominator (occiput/ sacrum) of presenting part to the quadrants of pelvis.</p>
<p>Eight positions are described</p>
<ul>
<li>When the denominator is directed towards symphysis pubis it gives a direct anterior position and when directed towards sacrum it gives direct posterior position</li>
<li>When denominator is directed towards the ileopectineal eminences, the position is left or right anterior position</li>
<li>If the denominator is directed towards the mid points of the ileopectineal line, it gives left or right anterior position</li>
<li>If the denominator is directed towards the left or light sacro-iliac joint then it is left or right posterior position</li>
</ul>
<p>Normal presentation is anterior position with commonest being left occipital anterior.</p>
<p>Left Occipito Posterior (LOP) - 3%
Left occipito lateral (LOL) - 40%
Left occipito anterior (LOA) - 15%
Right occipito anterior (ROA) - 10 %
Right occipito lateral (ROL) - 24%</p>
<p>Right occipito posterior (ROP) -</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="descent-and-engagement">DESCENT AND ENGAGEMENT<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#descent-and-engagement" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Refers to entry of the presenting part into the pelvis
Head is the presenting part in 99% of all labours
Descend is recorded in terms of the span of the foetal head still palpable in the abdomen above the level of symphysis pubis</p>
<p>The whole span of the head is subdivided into 5 fifths and each finger breaths spans 1 fith <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mn>5</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(1 / 5)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">1/5</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>When is completely free, the descend is <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>5</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mn>5</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">5 / 5</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">5/5</span></span></span></span></span> then to <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>4</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mn>5</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>3</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mn>5</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>2</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mn>5</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>1</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mn>5</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>0</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mn>5</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">4 / 5,3 / 5,2 / 5,1 / 5,0 / 5</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">4/5</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">3/5</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">2/5</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">1/5</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">0/5</span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<p>Once the widest diameter of foetal head has entered, only <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>2</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mn>5</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">2 / 5</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">2/5</span></span></span></span></span> is palpable and strictly speaking, this is when engagement has occurred</p>
<p>If a portion has sunk in the pelvis, pawlik's grip may not determine the identity of the presenting part.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="auscultation">AUSCULTATION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#auscultation" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>v Place the foetoscope on the back of the foetus, apply sufficient pressure to exclude external sounds
v Take note of foetal heart rate count and regularity.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="obstetric-vaginal-examination">OBSTETRIC VAGINAL EXAMINATION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#obstetric-vaginal-examination" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="indications">Indications:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#indications" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Ã¼ To confirm labour
Ã¼ Pelvic assessment
Ã¼ Assess progress of labour
Ã¼ Assessment of cervical ripening before induction of labour
Ã¼ Diagnose or rule out complications of labour</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="contraindications">Contraindications<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#contraindications" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="735a29e8">Ã¼ Suspected PROM<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#735a29e8" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Ã¼ Suspected placenta praevia.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="procedure">Procedure<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#procedure" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Ã¼ Explain the procedure to the patient
Ã¼ Let patient empty bladder
Ã¼ Provide privacy
Ã¼ Ensure adequate working space
Ã¼ Aseptic technique</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="inspection-of-the-external-genitalia">Inspection of the external genitalia<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#inspection-of-the-external-genitalia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Ã¼ Inspect for: scars, warts, scratch marks, varicose veins, hair distribution,
Ã¼ Any discharge - colour, consistency, smell, quantity,
Ã¼ State of urethral meatus</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="vulva-toilet">VULVA TOILET<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#vulva-toilet" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Ã¼ Aseptic technique - sterile gloving
Ã¼ Roll the sterile cotton wool swabs into five small balls and Soak them in a galipot containing antiseptic solution</p>
<p>Ã¼ Take them on the right hand, then drop one the left hand - swab with left hand the furthest labia majora from the top to the perineum. Similarly, swab the other side of labia majora.</p>
<p>Ã¼ Similarly, swab labia minora on both sides with the next two swabs using left hand.</p>
<p>Ã¼ Separate labia minora using your left hand then swab vestibule with the swab in the right hand from clitoris to fourchette using the right hand.</p>
<p>Ã¼ Drape the mother by placing the sterile towel under her buttocks and another one on the abdomen up to the hairline of the pubic area.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="speculum-examination-in-obstetric">SPECULUM EXAMINATION IN OBSTETRIC<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#speculum-examination-in-obstetric" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Read section on speculum examination below</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="digital-vaginal-examination">DIGITAL VAGINAL EXAMINATION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#digital-vaginal-examination" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Ã¼ Lubricate index and middle fingers of the right hand
Ã¼ Separate the labia with two fingers of the left hand
Ã¼ Insert index and middle finger of the right hand into the vaginal canal</p>
<ul>
<li>The terminal phalange of the middle finger is inserted first and pressed against the perineal body in order to relax introitus</li>
<li>The index finger is then slipped in and the two fingers are directed toward the cervix
Ã¼ Assess features at the cervix:</li>
<li>Dilatation of the cervix</li>
<li>Degree of thinning and softness (effacement)</li>
<li>Presence or absence of membranes</li>
<li>Confirm presenting part and its state eg moulding, caput</li>
<li>Direction of sutures and position of fontanels</li>
<li>Level of presenting part compared to the ischial spines
Ã¼ pelvic assessment</li>
<li>Feel for sacral promontory</li>
<li>Assess curvatures of the sacrum by sweeping your fingers downwards towards the outlet</li>
<li>Assess prominences of the ischial spines and tip of coccyx by sliding the examining fingers along the iscial spines and coccyx</li>
<li>Measure the sub-pubic angle by fitting the two examining fingers in the sub-pubic angle</li>
<li>Measure the inter-tuberous diameter by fitting the four knuckles of the examining hand between the ischial tuberosity.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="gynaecological-pelvic-examination">GYNAECOLOGICAL PELVIC EXAMINATION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#gynaecological-pelvic-examination" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="indication">Indication<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#indication" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="contraindication">Contraindication<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#contraindication" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="requirements">Requirements<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#requirements" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>

o Assignment: types of speculums and different sizes. How to examine patient using univalve speculums.
v Sterile gloves
v Non-sterile gloves
v Receiver with decontamination solution.
v chaperone, consent, good lighting</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="procedure">Procedure<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#procedure" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="preparation">Preparation<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#preparation" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>v Prepare environment for pelvic examination - privacy, equipment &amp; supplies
v Explain the procedure to the patient
v Patient empty bladder, remove underclothing, position in lithotomy
v Cover her to avoid unnecessary exposure</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="method-speculum-examination">Method: speculum examination<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#method-speculum-examination" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ol>
<li>Maintain infection prevention throughout the examination - wash hands, put on sterile gloves, use high-level disinfected / sterile instruments</li>
<li>Inspect external genitalia to screen for STI / FGM
v Warts, abnormal discharge, ulcers, bleeding from vagina, sores, swelling, presence and distribution of hair, obvious anatomical anomalies, female genital mutilation, cosmetics (eg rings)</li>
<li>Reassure the patient throughout the procedure</li>
<li>Choose speculum size for the patient</li>
<li>Warm blades under a stream of tepid water</li>
<li>Hold speculum in the right hand while the index finger of the left hand presses downwards on the fourchette to expose the introitus</li>
<li>Slide the closed blades obliquely (away from the urethral area and clitoris) over the fingers into the introitus, introduce the instrument into the vagina</li>
<li>While inserting the instrument rotate it to a clockwise direction until the anterior and posterior blades run along the anterior and posterior vaginal walls with the handles pointing towards the anus.</li>
<li>Open the blades to expose the cervix</li>
<li>Inspect cervix- erosion, colour, growths, friability, discharge,</li>
<li>Take lab specimens if necessary for investigation for PAP smear for cytology, vaginal secretions for microscopy.</li>
<li>Rotate the speculum and inspect vaginal wall for: warts, abnormal discharge, sores, bleeding</li>
<li>Remove the speculum gently in horizontal position and place it in decontamination solution.</li>
</ol>
<p>DIGITAL VAGINAL EXAMINATION IN GYNAECOLOGY
v Put on sterile gloves
v Clean the vulva
v Insert the index and middle fingers of right hand gently into the vaginal canal while you avoid touching clitoris with your thumb
v Examine the cervix:</p>
<p>Ã¼ Ostium- open or closed
Ã¼ Irregularity
Ã¼ Growth
Ã¼ Consistency
Ã¼ Mobility
Ã¼ Tenderness
v Examination of uterus - bimanual examination
Ã¼ Place your left hand on the abdomen, just above sympysis pubis
Ã¼ Locate uterus by feeling it between your left hand over abdomen and the finger tips of your right index and middle fingers placed on the cervix
Ã¼ Palpate for:
o size, shape and consistency, mobility,
o position : anteverted or retroverted</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="v-examination-of-the-adnexia">v Examination of the adnexia<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#v-examination-of-the-adnexia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Ã¼ locate the left fornix and place the finger tips in this fornix
Ã¼ together with left hand placed over the left side of lower abdomen, try to palpate for any mass or tenderness
Ã¼ repeat same on the right side
v Excitation of the cervix for endometritis
Ã¼ use your right index and middle fingers to gently move the cervix from left to right and check for any pain
v palpate the anterior, left and lateral walls of the vagina walls for: ruggae, growth, tenderness
v check vaginal muscle tone by asking the client to tighten vaginal muscle
v check for cystocele and rectocele
Ã¼ press the left index and middle finger downwards and ask patient to cough = rectocele</p>
<p>Ã¼ press the left index and middle finger upwards and ask patient to cough <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo>=</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">=</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.3669em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span></span></span></span></span> cystocele</p>
<ul>
<li>palpate bartholins glands on both sides of the labia majora</li>
<li>press on the trigone muscle to exclude cystitis</li>
<li>Milk the skenes glands with left hand.</li>
<li>Palpate the inguinal LN.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="examination-of-the-male-genitalia">EXAMINATION OF THE MALE GENITALIA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#examination-of-the-male-genitalia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="requirements">Requirements:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#requirements" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Ã¼ Gloves
Ã¼ Penlight
Inspection:
Ã¼ The pubic hair characteristics and distribution
Ã¼ The glans penis (retract the foreskin if patient uncircumcised):
o Colour
o Smegma
o External meatus of urethra
o Urethra discharge
Palpation:
Ã¼ The penis:
o Tenderness
o Induction
Ã¼ Strip the urethra for any discharge (you can ask the patient to perform this part of procedure for you:
o Firmly compress the base of the penis with your thumb and forefinger and move them towards the glans
o Press the glans penis between the thumb and forefinger
o Collect discharge</p>
<p>Scrotum and ventral surface of the penis:
Inspection:
Ã¼ Colour
Ã¼ Texture
Ã¼ Asymmetry
Ã¼ Unusual thickening
Ã¼ Presence of hernia
Ã¼ Trans - illuminate any masses in the scrotum
o When any mass is felt other than the testicle or spermatic cord determines whether it is filled with gas, fluid or solid material using penlight</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="palpation">Palpation:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#palpation" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>a. Inguinal canal for direct and indirect hernia
Ã¼ With patient standing, ask him to bear down as if having bowel movement
Ã¼ While he is straining inspect the areas of inguinal canal and the region of fossa ovalis
Ã¼ Ask patient to relax, insert the pulp of your examining finger into the lower part of the scrotum and carry it upward along vas deferens into the inguinal canal. (the finger depends on the size of the external ring which is normally palpable)
Ã¼ With your finger placed at the external ring ask the patient to cough and feel for a viscous mass against your finger (present if a hernia is present)
b. The testis, epididymitis, vasa deferentia
Ã¼ Use the thumb and first two fingers to assess:
i. Consistency
ii. Size
iii. Tenderness
iv. Fluid
v. Lumps or nodules
c. The inguinal lymph nodes</p>
<p>d. Cremasteric reflex
Ã¼ Elicit the cremasteric reflex bilaterally
Ã¼ Stroke the inner thigh with a blunt instrument such as the handle of the reflex hammer or with your finger
Ã¼ Normally the testicle and scrotum rise on the stroked side</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="examination-of-the-female-breast-and-axilla">EXAMINATION OF THE FEMALE BREAST AND AXILLA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#examination-of-the-female-breast-and-axilla" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Breast is an appendix of the skin in the milk-lines from axilla to groin.
The development has different stages - tanner's classification</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="preparation">Preparation<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#preparation" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Undress patient as far as waist, sits upright
It is necessary after examining the patient sitting upright to ask the patient to lie flat and reexamine the breasts</p>
<p>Both breasts must be exposed completely</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="method">Method<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#method" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="inspection">Inspection<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#inspection" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Ã˜ While patient in the following positions:
o Arms hanging loosely at the sides (arms aside)
o Arms held over head
o Arms held at hips
o Leading (bending) forward
Ã˜ Inspect each breast and compare them for:
o Size
o Symmetry
o Contour</p>
<ul>
<li>Skin colour</li>
<li>Venous pattern</li>
<li>Lesions</li>
<li>Inspect nipple for:</li>
<li>Size (compare both breast)</li>
<li>Retraction</li>
<li>Discharge</li>
<li>Ulceration</li>
<li>Inspect the areola for pigmentation</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="palpation">Palpation<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#palpation" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Systematically palpate the breast, axilla and supra-clavicular regions
Ask the patient to find first herself the lump and to point the lesion she has detected, before you attempt to do so and before you start palpation</p>
<p>Start with the normal breast to have her impression of the normal breast
Palpate the areola and nipple and finish with axilla</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="techniques">Techniques<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#techniques" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Two techniques:</p>
<ul>
<li>Palpation "with the flat of the hand"</li>
<li>Palpation "between the pulps of the fingers and the thumb"</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="flat-hand-technique">Flat-hand- technique:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#flat-hand-technique" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Exert a slight pressure on skin with the pulps of the middle and end phalanges of the fingers 2-5 and perform a small circular movement</li>
<li>Normal breast gives a firm lobulated impression with fine nodularity a feature particularly before the periods. In fat and after menopause expect to feel both lobulation and nodularity less easily</li>
<li>With flat-hand-technique accepted techiniques include:
Â§ Vertical zigzag palpation</li>
</ul>
<p>Â§ Concentric circular palpation
Â§ Quadrant palpation</p>
<ul>
<li>Most used technique is quadrant for clinician and self breast examination.
Ã˜ Perform palpation calmly, with patience, without skipping any part including axilla.
Ã˜ Palpation of areola:</li>
<li>Gently squeeze the areola skin between thumb and index together with a rolling movement (small retention cysts and glands of Montgomery can be noted as well as small centrally located tumours)</li>
<li>Indirectly by pressing with the top of index on different places of the areola, elicit nipple secretion, if present.
Ã˜ Palpation of nipple</li>
<li>Inform patient the procedure may hurt</li>
<li>Perform a short but firm squeeze of nipple between thumb and index finger</li>
<li>Notice secretion
Ã˜ Palpation of the tail of Spence and axillae</li>
<li>Palpate the tail as it enters axillae by gently compressing the tissue between the thumb and fingers
Ã˜ Palpation of the LN</li>
<li>With patient seated with arms flexed at elbow</li>
<li>Support the patient's right lower arm with your right hand to examine the right axilla &amp; vice varsa</li>
<li>Examine-apex, medial, lateral, anterior &amp; posterior.</li>
</ul>
<p>NB: Make always a well documented record of your examination
v Localization : name the quadrant or describe the location using "hours"
v Size: in mm or cm
v Shape: round - discoid - regular - irregular
v Consistency: very soft, soft, firm, hard, stony or bony hard
v Contour: in relation to surrounding tissue</p>
<p>v Tenderness: yes or no, spontaneous
v Mobility: in relation to the skin, breast tissue, fascia, thorax wall.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="common-investigations-in-reproductive-health-practice">COMMON INVESTIGATIONS IN REPRODUCTIVE HEALTH PRACTICE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#common-investigations-in-reproductive-health-practice" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Learning objectives</li>
<li></li>
</ul>
<p>ãƒ»</p>
<ul>
<li>At the end of the lecture, the student is expected to be able to:-</li>
<li>Know the scope of the common investigations in RHC</li>
<li>Acquire insight into the rational &amp; objective request for relevant investigations</li>
<li>Apply the same or similar investigations in different clinical situations</li>
<li>Interpret results of investigations for the benefit of patients</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="introduction-investigations">Introduction: Investigations<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#introduction-investigations" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Important aspect of patient management</li>
<li>Should always be rational/objective</li>
<li>Normal parameters should be known</li>
<li>Can be expensive</li>
<li>May be invasive</li>
<li>Supplement but not replace clinical acumen
"Good, comprehensive medical history &amp; physical examination remain key to paient management"</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="purpose-for-investigations">PURPOSE FOR INVESTIGATIONS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#purpose-for-investigations" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Confirmation of diagnosis</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Making diagnosis</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Estimate of disease severity</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Monitoring effect of treatment</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Monitoring recurrence</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Screening for disease</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="common-investigations-in-obstetrics">Common investigations in obstetrics<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#common-investigations-in-obstetrics" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="antenatal-care-anc">Antenatal care (ANC)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#antenatal-care-anc" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">H</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">b</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">]</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">&amp;</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">H</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">T</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\quad[\mathrm{Hb}] \&amp; \mathrm{HCT}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">Hb</span></span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mord">&amp;</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">HCT</span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li>To screen or confirm anemia</li>
<li>Forms a basis for supplementation</li>
<li>VDRL</li>
<li>Screening for syphylis - affects fetal outcome</li>
<li>Specific treponemal tests before treatment (e.g. TPHA)</li>
<li>Blood group</li>
<li>Establishes risk of feto-maternal incompartibility &amp; hemolytic disease</li>
<li>Prepares for transfusion needs</li>
<li>Urinalysis - Screening for protein, glycosuria, UTI, etc</li>
<li>HIV - PMTCT; Entry into prevention of transmission; Enables provision of support - psycho-social &amp; medical</li>
<li>Obstetric ultrasound - Appraisal of fetal growth; Fetal abnormality screening; Fetal well-being assessment: BPPS; Doppler studies; PET prediction</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="full-blood-count-fbc">Full blood count (FBC)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#full-blood-count-fbc" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Has multiplicity of value
Examples of significance:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">H</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">b</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">]</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">&amp;</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">H</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">T</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\quad[\mathrm{Hb}] \&amp; \mathrm{HCT}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">Hb</span></span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mord">&amp;</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">HCT</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Presence/absence of anemia; Etiology not implied</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Cell indices - MCV, NCH, MCHC - may allot anemia to broad categories:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Microcytic</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Hypochromic</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Megaloblastic</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Mixed</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>WBC count</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Total count</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Marked elevation - acute infections (bacterial/viral)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Moderate elevation - chronic infections</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Differential count</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Neutrophilia - acute bacterial infections</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Lymphocytosis -viral or chronic bacterial infections</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Peripheral blood film (PBF)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>RBC's</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Normocytic normochromic; hypochromic microcytic</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Polychromasia; reticulocytosis;megaloblasts</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Anisocytosis; poikilocytosis;tear drop cells</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Spherocytes; sickle forms</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>WBC,s</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Polymorphs - nuclear segmentation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Toxic granulation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Malaria parasites (MP,s)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Erythrocyte sedimentation rate</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>None specific</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>May indicate infection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Platelet count</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Absolute count/concentration</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="infections-in-pregnant-state">Infections in pregnant state<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#infections-in-pregnant-state" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ol>
<li>Urinary tract infections (UTI)</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Urinalysis:- appearanc; pH; blood; sugar; proteins; nitrites; urobilinogen; leukocytes; bilirubin; specific gravity; ketones</li>
<li>Microscopy:- pus cells; epithelial cells;casts; crystals; RBC,s; bacteria; yeast cells; trichomona vaginalis</li>
<li>Culture</li>
<li>sensitivity</li>
</ul>
<ol start="2">
<li>Respiratory tract infections</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>FBC; chest X-ray; sputum - AAFB,s</li>
</ul>
<ol start="3">
<li>Chorioamnionitis</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>FBC +ESR; vaginal swab - M/C/S</li>
</ul>
<ol start="4">
<li>Malaria</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>MP's</li>
</ul>
<ol start="5">
<li>Blood coagulation disorders -thrombo-embolic disease &amp; DIC</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Coagulation screen</li>
<li>Bleeding time; clotting time; APTT/KCCT; PTI/INR; platelet count</li>
<li>Thrombus localization</li>
<li>Doppler studies</li>
<li>Venography; radioisotope studies; thermography</li>
</ul>
<ol start="6">
<li>Hypertensive disease in pregnancy</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Renal function tests (RFT,s)</li>
<li>Urinalysis - protein, blood</li>
<li>U/E; uric acid; creatinine; creatinine clearance</li>
<li>Renal ultrasound</li>
<li>Liver function tests (LFT,s)</li>
<li>Bilirubin, liver enzymes</li>
<li>Coagulation screen; platelet count</li>
<li>Obstetric utrasound -FWB; doppler studies</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="7-value-of-ultrasound-in-obstetrics">7. Value of ultrasound in obstetrics<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#7-value-of-ultrasound-in-obstetrics" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Diagnosis of pregnancy</li>
<li>Intaruterine; extra-uterine</li>
<li>Fetal growth monitoring</li>
<li>Appropriateness of growth (AGA;SGA; LGA)</li>
<li>IUGR (asymmetrical; symmetrical)</li>
<li>Fetal weight, sex, viability</li>
<li>Fetal well-being</li>
<li>BPPS (fetal tone; fetal movements; respiratory movements; AF volume; placental echogenicity)</li>
<li>Pelvimetry</li>
<li>Gestation estimation-timing of specific epiphyseal plates' closure</li>
<li>Diagnosis of twins</li>
<li>Diagnosis of extra-uterine pregnancy</li>
</ul>
<ol start="8">
<li>Diabetes mellitus</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Urinalysis</li>
<li>Glycosuria; ketonuria; proteinuria</li>
<li>Blood sugar</li>
<li>RBS; FBS; OGTT; PPBS; Serial BS</li>
<li>Glycolysated Hb (Hb1c) - [N <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo>â‰¤</mo><mn>6</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">%</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\leq 6 \%</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7719em; vertical-align: -0.136em;"></span><span class="mrel">â‰¤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8056em; vertical-align: -0.0556em;"></span><span class="mord">6%</span></span></span></span></span> ]</li>
<li>Obstetric ultrasound - IUGR; Macrosomia; BPPS; Polyhydramnios; etc</li>
</ul>
<ol start="9">
<li>Rhesus isoimmunization</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Indirect Coombs test (ICT)</li>
<li>AF spectrophotometry -absobance deviation at 450nm</li>
<li>Cord blood at birth</li>
<li><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mi>H</mi><mi>b</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo><mo>+</mo><mi>h</mi><mi>c</mi><mi>t</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">[H b]+h c t</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.08125em;">H</span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">h</span><span class="mord mathnormal">c</span><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li>Direct Coombs test</li>
<li>Bilirubin</li>
</ul>
<ol start="10">
<li>Anemia &amp; Antepartum hemorrhage</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Anemia</li>
<li><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>F</mi><mi>B</mi><mi>C</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>P</mi><mi>B</mi><mi>F</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">F B C+P B F</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">FBC</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">PBF</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li>Stool o/c</li>
<li>MPs</li>
<li>Antepartum hemorrhage (APH)</li>
<li>Placental localization</li>
<li>Ultrasound; EUA</li>
<li>Coagulation screen</li>
<li><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mi>H</mi><mi>b</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>h</mi><mi>c</mi><mi>t</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">[H b]=h c t</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.08125em;">H</span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">h</span><span class="mord mathnormal">c</span><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
<ol start="11">
<li>Antepartum hemorrhage (APH); Establishment of fetal maturity</li>
</ol>
<p>Septicemia &amp; endotoxic shock</p>
<ul>
<li>RFTs including urine output</li>
<li>Blood cultures</li>

</ul>
<p>Establishment of fetal maturity</p>
<ul>
<li>Amniocentesis</li>
<li>Surfactant or 'shake' test</li>
<li>Lecithin:sphingomyelin (L/S) ratio ( <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>â‰¥</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>:</mo><mn>2</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">N \geq 1: 2</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8193em; vertical-align: -0.136em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">N</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">â‰¥</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">:</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span></span></span></span></span> )</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="common-investigations-in-gynaecology">Common investigations in Gynaecology<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#common-investigations-in-gynaecology" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
